CREATE TABLE Iller (
    IlID INT PRIMARY KEY,
    IlAdi NVARCHAR(50),
    Koordinat GEOGRAPHY
);

-- Bütün iller arasındaki mesafeleri bulan sorgu
DECLARE @AnkaraIlID INT = (SELECT IlID FROM Iller WHERE IlAdi = 'Ankara');
SELECT
    A.IlAdi AS Il1,
    B.IlAdi AS Il2,
    A.Koordinat.STDistance(B.Koordinat) / 1000 AS DistanceKm
FROM
    Iller A
CROSS JOIN
    Iller B
WHERE
    A.IlID <> B.IlID;
